Notice

WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
B. Anandaraj, A Male Child Born to K. Balaraman on 5-3-1993 Residing at No. 10/16, Mosque Street, Royapuram,
Chennai-600 013, has been Living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment sugery by Dr. Kannan this has
been confirmed by Dr. Jayaraman, MS, MCH, MNAMS, Dip.N.B, PhD., FICS of Kilpauk Medical College and Hospital,
Chennai-600 010, Regn. No. 32070 By This I, May be Treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as B. CINDY.

Chennai,
13th June 2014.

B. ANANDARAJ.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

Mr. P. Bharath Raja was born as a male child of C. Petchi Muthu on 6-3-1983 residing at 154A/NA, Aravanigal
2nd Street, Nadarajapuram, Pukkathurai-603 308. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been living as
a female (Reference Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS, Mch, MNAMS, Dip, NB, Phd., FICS, Professor Head Department of Burns,
Plastic & Reconstructive Surgery, Government Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010.) the through Clinical
Examination under Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS, Mch, MNAMS, Dip, NB, Phd., FICS, shows that I could be treated as a female,
P. Bharath Raja shall be known as P. BHARATHI.

Kancheepuram,
13th June 2014.

P. BHARATH RAJA.

Chetty Thottam, Royapuram, Chennai-600 013, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment
sugery by Dr. Nagaraj. This has been confirmed by Dr. V. Jayaraman, Ms, Mch, MNAMS, Dip. N.B., Phd., FICS of Kilpauk
Medical College & Hospital, Chennai-600 010, Regn. No. 32070 by This I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth
be known as G. SOWNDHARYA.

Chennai,

A.G. CHINNABALU.
